<P id=PARA2 style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P id=PARA4 style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">JAMES G. RAKES, CHAIRMAN, PRESIDENT &amp; CEO </FONT></P>
<P id=PARA5 style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">(540) 951-6236&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>jrakes@nbbank.com</U></FONT></P>
<P id=PARA6 style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">DAVID K. SKEENS, TREASURER &amp; CFO</FONT></P>
<P id=PARA7 style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">(540) 951-6347&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>dskeens@nbbank.com</U></FONT></P>
<P id=PARA8 style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>
<P id=PARA9 style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif"><U><B>NATIONAL BANKSHARES, INC. REPORTS</B></U></FONT></P>
<P id=PARA10 style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif"><U><B>SECOND QUARTER AND FIRST HALF EARNINGS</B></U><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>
<P id=PARA11 style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P id=PARA12 style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">BLACKSBURG, VA, JULY 23, 2015:&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>National Bankshares, Inc. </B>(NASDAQ Capital Market:&nbsp;<B>NKSH</B>) today announced its results of operations for the second quarter and first half of 2015. The Company reported</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif"> net income of almost $8.08 million for the six months ended June 30, 2015 compared to $8.51 million at June 30, 2014. Basic earnings per share were $1.16 at June 30, 2015 compared to $1.23 for the same period in 2014. For the first half of the year, the return on average assets was 1.41% and the return on average equity was 9.55% compared to 1.54% and 11.22%, respectively, for the first six months of 2014. At June 30, 2015, the Company had total assets of almost $1.15 billion which was an increase of 1.75% when compared to $1.13 billion at the end of June 2014.</FONT></P>
<P id=PARA14 style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 0pt; MARGIN-TOP: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P id=PARA15 style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">Commenting on the Company&#8217;s financial results, National Bankshares Chairman, President &amp; CEO James G. Rakes said, &#8220;Loan growth of over $33.54 million, or 5.65%, from June 30, 2014 is a positive indicator of a stronger demand for credit. We continue to focus on meeting the financial needs of our customers and our employees are dedicated to striving to meet those needs</FONT><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">.&#8221;</FONT></P>
<P id=PARA16 style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P id=PARA17 style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">National Bankshares, Inc., headquartered in Blacksburg, Virginia, is the parent company of The National Bank of Blacksburg, which does business as National Bank, and of National Bankshares Financial Services, Inc.&nbsp;&nbsp;National Bank is a community bank operating from 26 offices throughout Southwest Virginia.&nbsp;National Bankshares Financial Services, Inc. is an investment and insurance subsidiary in the same trade area.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company&#8217;s stock is traded on the NASDAQ Capital Market under the symbol &#8220;NKSH.&#8221;&nbsp;Additional information is available at <U>www.nationalbankshares.com</U>.</FONT></P>
<P id=PARA18 style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P id=PARA19 style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25"><FONT style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, Times, serif">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
